	ACW_recruit_alabama = {
		icon = us_flag
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				is_acw_tag = yes
			}
		}
		highlight_state_targets = {
			state = 367
		}
		available = {
			controls_state = 367

		}
		visible = {
			367 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { has_state_flag = ACW_recruited_@ROOT }

			NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
			OR = {
				country_exists = CSA

		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 12
		cost = 0

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 14
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				367 = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = COR
				NOT = { has_global_flag = KR_no_unit_limits }
				set_temp_variable = { check_value = num_divisions }
				add_to_temp_variable = { check_value = 4 }
				check_variable = { check_value > max_divisions }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = TEX
				NOT = { has_global_flag = KR_no_unit_limits }
				set_temp_variable = { check_value = num_divisions }
				add_to_temp_variable = { check_value = 3 }
				check_variable = { check_value > max_divisions }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = KR_no_unit_limits
					tag = TEX
					tag = COR
				}
				set_temp_variable = { check_value = num_divisions }
				add_to_temp_variable = { check_value = 2 }
				check_variable = { check_value > max_divisions }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					is_federal_tag = yes

		}

	ACW_recruit_north_arkansas = {
		icon = us_flag
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				is_acw_tag = yes
			}
		}
		highlight_state_targets = {
			state = 1156
		}
		available = {
			controls_state = 1156
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ACW_is_recruiting }
		}
		visible = {
			1156 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { has_state_flag = ACW_recruited_@ROOT }
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
			OR = {
				country_exists = CSA
				country_exists = TEX
				country_exists = CAL
				has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}

		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 12
		cost = 0

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 9
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				1156 = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = COR
				NOT = { has_global_flag = KR_no_unit_limits }
				set_temp_variable = { check_value = num_divisions }
				add_to_temp_variable = { check_value = 2 }
				check_variable = { check_value > max_divisions }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = KR_no_unit_limits
					tag = COR
				}
				set_temp_variable = { check_value = num_divisions }
				add_to_temp_variable = { check_value = 1 }
				check_variable = { check_value > max_divisions }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					is_federal_tag = yes
					has_country_flag = choice_made
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision ACW_recruit_north_arkansas"
			set_country_flag = ACW_is_recruiting
			1156 = { set_state_flag = ACW_recruiting_@ROOT }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove ACW_recruit_north_arkansas"
			clr_country_flag = ACW_is_recruiting
			1156 = {
				clr_state_flag = ACW_recruiting_@ROOT
				set_state_flag = ACW_recruited_@ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_federal_tag = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ACW_recruit_1_unit
				hidden_effect = {
					1156 = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"1st Northern Arkansas Loyalists\" division_template = \"Loyalist Militia\"  start_experience_factor = 0.0"
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = CSA
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ACW_recruit_1_unit
				hidden_effect = {
					1156 = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"1st Northern Arkansas Revolutionary Militia\" division_template = \"Revolutionary Militia\"  start_experience_factor = 0.0"
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes

	ACW_recruit_wisconsin = {
		icon = us_flag
		allowed = {
			OR = {
				is_acw_tag = yes
			}
		}
		highlight_state_targets = {
			state = 394
		}
		available = {
			controls_state = 394
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ACW_is_recruiting }
		}
		visible = {
			394 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { has_state_flag = ACW_recruited_@ROOT }
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag }
			OR = {
				country_exists = CSA
				country_exists = TEX
				country_exists = CAL
				has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag
			}
		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		}

		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 12
		cost = 0

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				394 = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = TEX
				NOT = { has_global_flag = KR_no_unit_limits }
				set_temp_variable = { check_value = num_divisions }
				add_to_temp_variable = { check_value = 2 }
				check_variable = { check_value > max_divisions }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = KR_no_unit_limits
					tag = TEX
				}
				set_temp_variable = { check_value = num_divisions }
				add_to_temp_variable = { check_value = 1 }
				check_variable = { check_value > max_divisions }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					is_federal_tag = yes
					has_country_flag = choice_made
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision ACW_recruit_wisconsin"
			set_country_flag = ACW_is_recruiting
			394 = { set_state_flag = ACW_recruiting_@ROOT }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove ACW_recruit_wisconsin"
			clr_country_flag = ACW_is_recruiting
			394 = {
				clr_state_flag = ACW_recruiting_@ROOT
				set_state_flag = ACW_recruited_@ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_federal_tag = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ACW_recruit_1_unit
				hidden_effect = {
					394 = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"1st Western Wisconsin Loyalists\" division_template = \"Loyalist Militia\"  start_experience_factor = 0.0"
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = CSA
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ACW_recruit_1_unit
				hidden_effect = {
					394 = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"1st Western Wisconsin Revolutionary Militia\" division_template = \"Revolutionary Militia\"  start_experience_factor = 0.0"
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}

				hidden_effect = {
					394 = {
